***invallen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:invallen.html>invallen</a> (11202)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">in</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">in</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vallen.html>vallen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fall</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:invallen.html>invallen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Plural form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:inval.html>inval</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:invallen.html>invallen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to fall into</li>
<li>to begin abruptly, to suddenly start appearing</li>
<li>to fill in (e.g. for someone who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sick)
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:val.html>val</a> in</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zieke.html>zieke</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:collega.html>collega</a>.</i>: I am filling in for a sick colleague.</dd></dl></li>
<li>to strike
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:licht.html>licht</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:valt.html>valt</a> in</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:onder.html>onder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoek.html>hoek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> 40 <a href = vnd.unilang:graden.html>graden</a>.</i>: The light <a href = vnd.unilang:strikes.html>strikes</a> at an angle of 40 degrees.</dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:inval.html>inval</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">incidence</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-s-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoek.html>hoek</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">angle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> investigation (1499)</h1><br><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
